Service: TheHolyBible
Service Documentation: The APIs in this service provide access to the entire American Standard edition of the Holy Bible. This web service is provided free by Francis Shanahan.
Port: TheHolyBibleSoap
Port Documentation: 
 Operation: ListBooks
 Operation Documentation: Lists the books of the Bible, the ids returned can be used in subsequent function calls to limit your results to that book.
  Input Parameter: ListBooksSoapIn
  Input Parameter Documentation: 
   ListBooks (complexType)
  Output Parameter: ListBooksSoapOut
  Output Parameter Documentation: 
   ListBooksResponse (complexType)
   ListBooksResult ()
 Operation: GetContentByChapterVerse
 Operation Documentation: Returns content based on matching Chapters and Verse parameters. Matching content from all books is returned.
  Input Parameter: GetContentByChapterVerseSoapIn
  Input Parameter Documentation: 
   GetContentByChapterVerse (complexType)
   chapter (int)
   verse (int)
  Output Parameter: GetContentByChapterVerseSoapOut
  Output Parameter Documentation: 
   GetContentByChapterVerseResponse (complexType)
   GetContentByChapterVerseResult ()
 Operation: GetChapters
 Operation Documentation: Lists all chapters in a book.
  Input Parameter: GetChaptersSoapIn
  Input Parameter Documentation: 
   GetChapters (complexType)
   book (int)
  Output Parameter: GetChaptersSoapOut
  Output Parameter Documentation: 
   GetChaptersResponse (complexType)
   GetChaptersResult ()
 Operation: GetContentByBookChapterVerse
 Operation Documentation: Gets a specific verse from a specific book and chapter.
  Input Parameter: GetContentByBookChapterVerseSoapIn
  Input Parameter Documentation: 
   GetContentByBookChapterVerse (complexType)
   book (int)
   chapter (int)
   verse (int)
  Output Parameter: GetContentByBookChapterVerseSoapOut
  Output Parameter Documentation: 
   GetContentByBookChapterVerseResponse (complexType)
   GetContentByBookChapterVerseResult ()
 Operation: GetContentByBookChapter
 Operation Documentation: Gets all verses in a given chapter and book.
  Input Parameter: GetContentByBookChapterSoapIn
  Input Parameter Documentation: 
   GetContentByBookChapter (complexType)
   book (int)
   chapter (int)
  Output Parameter: GetContentByBookChapterSoapOut
  Output Parameter Documentation: 
   GetContentByBookChapterResponse (complexType)
   GetContentByBookChapterResult ()
